ENTRY       EC 2.1.1.228                Enzyme
NAME        tRNA (guanine37-N1)-methyltransferase;
            TrmD;
            tRNA (m1G37) methyltransferase;
            transfer RNA (m1G37) methyltransferase;
            Trm5p;
            TRMT5;
            tRNA-(N1G37) methyltransferase;
            MJ0883 (gene name)
CLASS       Transferases;
            Transferring one-carbon groups;
            Methyltransferases
SYSNAME     S-adenosyl-L-methionine:tRNA (guanine37-N1)-methyltransferase
REACTION    S-adenosyl-L-methionine + guanine37 in tRNA = S-adenosyl-L-homocysteine + N1-methylguanine37 in tRNA [RN:R00597]
ALL_REAC    R00597
SUBSTRATE   S-adenosyl-L-methionine [CPD:C00019];
            guanine37 in tRNA
PRODUCT     S-adenosyl-L-homocysteine [CPD:C00021];
            N1-methylguanine37 in tRNA
COMMENT     This enzyme is important for the maintenance of the correct reading frame during translation. Unlike TrmD from Escherichia coli, which recognizes the G36pG37 motif preferentially, the human enzyme (encoded by TRMT5) also methylates inosine at position 37 [4].
HISTORY     EC 2.1.1.228 created 2011 (EC 2.1.1.31 created 1971, part transferred 2011 to EC 2.1.1.228)
